<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Piano Concerto No.4
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ru">Концерт для фортепиано с оркестром № 4 (Бетховен)</span>; <span title="fr">Concerto pour piano nº 4 de Beethoven</span>; <span title="en">Piano Concerto No. 4</span>; <span title="zh">第4號鋼琴協奏曲 (貝多芬)</span>; <span title="sr">IV Klavirski Koncert (Betoven)</span>; <span class="expandline" title="13 more..."><span title="ca">Concert per a piano núm. 4 (Beethoven)</span>; <span title="de">4. Klavierkonzert</span>; <span title="it">Concerto per pianoforte e orchestra n. 4</span>; <span title="pl">IV koncert fortepianowy Beethovena</span>; <span title="uk">Концерт для фортепіано з оркестром № 4 (Бетховен)</span>; <span title="sl">Klavirski koncert št. 4 (Beethoven)</span>; <span title="fi">Pianokonsertto nro 4 (Beethoven)</span>; <span title="nl">Pianoconcert nr. 4</span>; <span title="ja">ピアノ協奏曲第4番 (ベートーヴェン)</span>; <span title="es">Concierto para piano n.º 4 (Beethoven)</span>; <span title="ro">Concertul pentru pian nr. 4 (Beethoven)</span>; <span title="hu">Beethoven: 4. zongoraverseny</span>; <span title="el">Κονσέρτο για πιάνο Νο.4</span></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
